---
 layout: post
 title: 几种颜色映射方案的解析式
 categories:
 - 科
 tags:
 - 颜色
---

- 2016年09月02日 21:43:51 初稿
- 2017年02月23日 20:30:43 补充代码

在做三维数据的填色表面图时, 需要使用颜色映射方案, 将一定范围内的数值映射成一定的颜色来显示. 可用的颜色映射方案很多很多, 但并不是所有的方案都适合用来展示数据. 我前面有篇博文[数据展示：请选择好的颜色映射方案](http://jerkwin.github.io/2014/11/20/%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E5%B1%95%E7%A4%BA-%E8%AF%B7%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E5%A5%BD%E7%9A%84%E9%A2%9C%E8%89%B2%E6%98%A0%E5%B0%84%E6%96%B9%E6%A1%88/)对此有些说明, 可做参考.

在这篇博文中, 我首先推荐一篇有关颜色设计的资料[Good Colour Maps: How to Design Them](http://peterkovesi.com/projects/colourmaps/ColourmapTheory/index.html), 供需要使用颜色映射的人参考.

传统的颜色映射方案, 给出的都是一定范围内的离散数据, 使用中有时需要进行插值, 不是很方便在程序中使用. 一种解决办法是将其拟合成解析表达式. 拟合时, 我们一般使用比较简单的函数, 如高斯函数, 二次, 三次函数等. 下面我给出一些常用颜色映射方案解析表达式的拟合结果.

下面是几种常见常用的颜色映射图, 大家可根据自己的需要来选.

![](https://jerkwin.github.io/pic/colormap_all.png)

### 网络资料

- [gnuplot颜色映射方案说明](http://blog.sciencenet.cn/blog-373392-517857.html)
- [gnuplot各种颜色方案](https://github.com/bruceravel/Graphics-Gnuplot-Palettes)
- [matlab的parula方案](http://tex.stackexchange.com/questions/232690/color-coded-plots-with-colorbar-in-pgfplots) [fake parula](https://github.com/BIDS/colormap/blob/master/fake_parula.py)
- [python matplotlib的viridis方案](http://medvis.org/2016/02/23/better-than-the-rainbow-the-matplotlib-alternative-colormaps/)
- [最简单的彩虹方案](http://stackoverflow.com/questions/7706339)

[gnuplot所用的颜色映射公式](http://juluribk.com/2011/05/18/843/)

	* there are 37 available rgb color mapping formulae:
	         0: 0               1: 0.5             2: 1
	         3: x               4: x^2             5: x^3
	         6: x^4             7: sqrt(x)         8: sqrt(sqrt(x))
	         9: sin(90x)       10: cos(90x)       11: |x-0.5|
	        12: (2x-1)^2       13: sin(180x)      14: |cos(180x)|
	        15: sin(360x)      16: cos(360x)      17: |sin(360x)|
	        18: |cos(360x)|    19: |sin(720x)|    20: |cos(720x)|
	        21: 3x             22: 3x-1           23: 3x-2
	        24: |3x-1|         25: |3x-2|         26: (3x-1)/2
	        27: (3x-2)/2       28: |(3x-1)/2|     29: |(3x-2)/2|
	        30: x/0.32-0.78125 31: 2*x-0.84       32: 4x;1;-2x+1.84;x/0.08-11.5
	        33: |2*x - 0.5|    34: 2*x            35: 2*x - 0.5
	        36: 2*x - 1
	      * negative numbers mean inverted=negative colour component
	      * thus the ranges in `set pm3d rgbformulae` are -36..36

<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">fit</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">       </span><span style="color: #00A000">g</span>(x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="border: 1px solid #FF0000">$</span>data<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">u</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">12:13</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">via</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Y0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>A<span style="color: #666666">,</span>x0<span style="color: #666666">,</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">w</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">print</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">sprintf</span>(<span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;r=Gauss(%12.6f,%12.6f,%12.6f,%12.6f)</span><span style="color: #BB6622; font-weight: bold">\n</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;</span><span style="color: #666666">,</span>Y0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>A<span style="color: #666666">,</span>x0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>w)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">fit</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">       </span><span style="color: #00A000">g</span>(x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="border: 1px solid #FF0000">$</span>data<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">u</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">12:15</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">via</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Y0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>A<span style="color: #666666">,</span>x0<span style="color: #666666">,</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">w</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">print</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">sprintf</span>(<span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;b=Gauss(%12.6f,%12.6f,%12.6f,%12.6f)</span><span style="color: #BB6622; font-weight: bold">\n</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;</span><span style="color: #666666">,</span>Y0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>A<span style="color: #666666">,</span>x0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>w)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">fit</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>[<span style="color: #666666">:.5</span>]<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">g</span>(x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="border: 1px solid #FF0000">$</span>data<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">u</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">12:14</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">via</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Y0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>A<span style="color: #666666">,</span>x0<span style="color: #666666">,</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">w</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">print</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">sprintf</span>(<span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;g=Gauss(%12.6f,%12.6f,%12.6f,%12.6f)</span><span style="color: #BB6622; font-weight: bold">\n</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;</span><span style="color: #666666">,</span>Y0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>A<span style="color: #666666">,</span>x0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>w)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #B8860B">Y0</span><span style="color: #666666">=1</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #B8860B">A</span><span style="color: #666666">=-1</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #B8860B">x0</span><span style="color: #666666">=2</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #B8860B">w</span><span style="color: #666666">=0.5</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">fit</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>[<span style="color: #666666">.5:</span>]<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">g</span>(x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="border: 1px solid #FF0000">$</span>data<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">u</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">12:14</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">via</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Y0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>A<span style="color: #666666">,</span>x0<span style="color: #666666">,</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">w</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">print</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">sprintf</span>(<span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;g=Gauss(%12.6f,%12.6f,%12.6f,%12.6f)</span><span style="color: #BB6622; font-weight: bold">\n</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;</span><span style="color: #666666">,</span>Y0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>A<span style="color: #666666">,</span>x0<span style="color: #666666">,</span>w)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">p</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>[]<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>[<span style="color: #666666">0:1</span>]<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="border: 1px solid #FF0000">$</span>data<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">u</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">12:14</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">w</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>p<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>pt<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">7,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">g</span>(x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">w</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>l<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>lw<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">2</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
</pre></div>
</td></tr></table>

<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">import</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #0000FF; font-weight: bold">math</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">def</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">Cubic</span>(y0,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>a1,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>a2,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>a3,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x):<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">return</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>y0<span style="color: #666666">+</span>a1<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">+</span>a2<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">+</span>a3<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">def</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">Gauss</span>(y0,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>A,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x0,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>w,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x):<span style="color: #bbbbbb">   </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">return</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>y0<span style="color: #666666">+</span>A<span style="color: #666666">*</span>math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>exp(<span style="color: #666666">-.5*</span>(x<span style="color: #666666">-</span>x0)<span style="color: #666666">**2/</span>w<span style="color: #666666">**2</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">def</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #00A000">RGB</span>(V,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vmin<span style="color: #666666">=0</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vmax<span style="color: #666666">=1</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vcnt<span style="color: #666666">=0.5</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm<span style="color: #666666">=8</span>):<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span>x<span style="color: #666666">=</span>(V<span style="color: #666666">-</span>Vmin)<span style="color: #666666">/</span>(Vmax<span style="color: #666666">-</span>Vmin)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">if</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>V<span style="color: #666666">&lt;</span>Vcnt:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x<span style="color: #666666">=0.5*</span>(V<span style="color: #666666">-</span>Vmin)<span style="color: #666666">/</span>(Vcnt<span style="color: #666666">-</span>Vmin)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">else</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span>x<span style="color: #666666">=0.5*</span>(V<span style="color: #666666">-</span>Vcnt)<span style="color: #666666">/</span>(Vmax<span style="color: #666666">-</span>Vcnt)<span style="color: #666666">+0.5</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">if</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm<span style="color: #666666">==1</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">Rainbow</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">http://stackoverflow.com/questions/7706339</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=1</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>g<span style="color: #666666">=1</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=1</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">if</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">   </span>x<span style="color: #666666">&lt;0.25</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>r<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">0</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb">     </span>g<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">4*</span>x<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">elif</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x<span style="color: #666666">&lt;0.50</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>r<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">0</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb">     </span>b<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">2-4*</span>x<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">elif</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x<span style="color: #666666">&lt;0.75</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>r<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">4*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">-2</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>b<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">0</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">else</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb">        </span>g<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">4-4*</span>x;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>b<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">0</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">elif</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm<span style="color: #666666">==2</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">Rainbow</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">gnuplot_33/13/10</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">abs</span>(<span style="color: #666666">2*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">-0.5</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>g<span style="color: #666666">=</span>math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>sin(math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>pi<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=</span>math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>cos(<span style="color: #666666">.5*</span>math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>pi<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">elif</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm<span style="color: #666666">==3</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">Rainbow</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">gnuplot_26/13/10</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=</span>(<span style="color: #666666">3*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">-1</span>)<span style="color: #666666">/2</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>g<span style="color: #666666">=</span>math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>sin(math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>pi<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=</span>math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>cos(<span style="color: #666666">.5*</span>math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>pi<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">elif</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm<span style="color: #666666">==4</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">Rainbow</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">gnuplot_22/13/-31</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=3*</span>x<span style="color: #666666">-1</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>g<span style="color: #666666">=</span>math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>sin(math<span style="color: #666666">.</span>pi<span style="color: #666666">*</span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=0.84-2*</span>x<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">elif</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm<span style="color: #666666">==5</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">Rainbow</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">rainbow_bgyr_35-85_c72_n256</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">if</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">   </span>x<span style="color: #666666">&lt;.137254902</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=0</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">b=Gauss(</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">          </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">-0.058369,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">   </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">1.059922,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">0.287974,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">0.397540,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">x)</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">g=Gauss(</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">          </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">-0.704876,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">   </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">1.571408,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">0.517821,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">0.546999,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">x)</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">if</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">x&gt;0.5:</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">g=Gauss(</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">1.049701,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">-11.064245,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">2.617332,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">0.736066,</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">x)</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Cubic(<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span><span style="color: #666666">0.231337</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">1.075890</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">1.311415</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-1.847011</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>g<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Cubic(<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span><span style="color: #666666">0.298328</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">1.762637</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-0.350029</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-1.819830</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Cubic(<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span><span style="color: #666666">0.751440</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">1.685291</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-2.782078</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-0.283025</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">if</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x<span style="color: #666666">&gt;0.5</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Cubic(<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-0.671865</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">5.184908</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-4.640348</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">0.831930</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span>g<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Cubic(<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">1.155680</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-0.818882</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">1.293472</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-1.569916</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Cubic(<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">1.148734</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">0.728630</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">-3.447502</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #666666">1.721348</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>x)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">min</span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">max</span>(r,<span style="color: #666666">0</span>),<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">1</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span>g<span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">min</span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">max</span>(g,<span style="color: #666666">0</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>,<span style="color: #666666">1</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">min</span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">max</span>(b,<span style="color: #666666">0</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>,<span style="color: #666666">1</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">return</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>r,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>g,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>b<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

Vmin<span style="color: #666666">=-0.008</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vmax<span style="color: #666666">=0.015</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vcnt<span style="color: #666666">=0</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>dV<span style="color: #666666">=0.0001</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm<span style="color: #666666">=8</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
Nbin<span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">int</span>((Vmax<span style="color: #666666">-</span>Vmin)<span style="color: #666666">/</span>dV)<span style="color: #666666">+1</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">颜色标尺</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
Nx<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Nbin;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Ny<span style="color: #666666">=70</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>
w1<span style="color: #666666">=5</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span>w2<span style="color: #666666">=3</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span>w3<span style="color: #666666">=2</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
h1<span style="color: #666666">=20</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>h2<span style="color: #666666">=10</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>h3<span style="color: #666666">=5</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF">file</span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">open</span>(<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>ColorMap<span style="color: #666666">-</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">str</span>(cm)<span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #666666">.</span>ppm<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>w<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF">file</span><span style="color: #666666">.</span>write(<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>P3\n<span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#ppm\n&#39;+str(Nx)+&#39;</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">&#39;+str(Ny)+&#39;\n255\n&#39;)</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">for</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>j<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">in</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">range</span>(Ny):<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">for</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>i<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">in</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">range</span>(Nx):<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">if</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>i<span style="color: #666666">&gt;</span>w1<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">and</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>i<span style="color: #666666">&lt;</span>Nx<span style="color: #666666">-</span>w1<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">and</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>(<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>\<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">       </span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">abs</span>(i<span style="color: #666666">-100*</span>(i<span style="color: #666666">/100</span>))<span style="color: #666666">&lt;</span>w1<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">and</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>(j<span style="color: #666666">&lt;</span>h1<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">or</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>j<span style="color: #666666">&gt;</span>Ny<span style="color: #666666">-</span>h1))<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>\<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">or</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">abs</span>(i<span style="color: #666666">-</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">50*</span>(i<span style="color: #666666">/</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">50</span>))<span style="color: #666666">&lt;</span>w2<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">and</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>(j<span style="color: #666666">&lt;</span>h2<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">or</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>j<span style="color: #666666">&gt;</span>Ny<span style="color: #666666">-</span>h2))<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>\<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">or</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">abs</span>(i<span style="color: #666666">-</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">10*</span>(i<span style="color: #666666">/</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">10</span>))<span style="color: #666666">&lt;</span>w3<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">and</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>(j<span style="color: #666666">&lt;</span>h3<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">or</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>j<span style="color: #666666">&gt;</span>Ny<span style="color: #666666">-</span>h3))<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>):<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span>r<span style="color: #666666">=0</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>g<span style="color: #666666">=0</span>;<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=0</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">else</span>:<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span>V<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Vmin<span style="color: #666666">+</span>i<span style="color: #666666">*</span>dV<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">      </span>r,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>g,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=</span>RGB(V,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vmin,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vmax,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vcnt,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">    </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">file</span><span style="color: #666666">.</span>write(<span style="color: #AA22FF">str</span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">int</span>(r<span style="color: #666666">*255</span>))<span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">str</span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">int</span>(g<span style="color: #666666">*255</span>))<span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">str</span>(<span style="color: #AA22FF">int</span>(b<span style="color: #666666">*255</span>))<span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">file</span><span style="color: #666666">.</span>write(<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>\n<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF">file</span><span style="color: #666666">.</span>close()<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>

<span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">#</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #008800; font-style: italic">调色板</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF">file</span><span style="color: #666666">=</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">open</span>(<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>ColorMap<span style="color: #666666">-</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #AA22FF">str</span>(cm)<span style="color: #666666">+</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span><span style="color: #666666">.</span>pal<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>w<span style="color: #BB4444">&#39;</span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">for</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>i<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF; font-weight: bold">in</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">range</span>(Nx):<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span>V<span style="color: #666666">=</span>Vmin<span style="color: #666666">+</span>i<span style="color: #666666">*</span>dV<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span>r,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>g,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>b<span style="color: #666666">=</span>RGB(V,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vmin,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vmax,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>Vcnt,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>cm)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #bbbbbb">  </span><span style="color: #AA22FF">file</span><span style="color: #666666">.</span>write(<span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;</span><span style="color: #BB6688; font-weight: bold">%10.6f</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #BB6688; font-weight: bold">%10.6f</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #BB6688; font-weight: bold">%10.6f</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #BB6688; font-weight: bold">%10.6f</span><span style="color: #BB6622; font-weight: bold">\n</span><span style="color: #BB4444">&quot;</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span><span style="color: #666666">%</span><span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>(V,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>r,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>g,<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>b)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"> </span>)<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
<span style="color: #AA22FF">file</span><span style="color: #666666">.</span>close()<span style="color: #bbbbbb"></span>
</pre></div>
